| <span data-ttu-id="48f1a-1784">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="48f1a-1784">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="48f1a-1785">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="48f1a-1785">Value</span></span> |
